Anomalous gold also occurs in zones of local silicification, argillic alteration, and quartz-alunite veining.",The deposit is pervasively oxidized.,WBG deposit (Wall Street-Black Hawk-Gracey),Ore is associated with shear zones dating from a period of regional extensional faulting about 15-10 Ma.,"LaPointe, D.D., Schruben, Paul G.","""Nelson Monzonite"", ""Patsy Mine Volcanics""","Monzonite,Mafic Intrusive Rock,Andesite,Dacite",,"Gneiss,Schist","The northern Eldorado Mountains are characterized by many west-dipping listric normal faults which sole into a west-dipping detachment, all formed about between 15 and 10 Ma due to regional extension. The structural style changes markedly in the southern Eldorado Mountains, where Tertiary volcanic strata dip west and are cut by east-dipping listric faults.  The Eldorado Canyon and mining district are located between the two structurally distinct areas and represent an ?accommodation zone?., The deposit is bounded on all sides by post-mineral, high-angle faults.",The deposit is situated within a probable structural ?accommodation zone? marking the boundary between different styles of faulting in the northern El Dorado mountains and the southern portion of the range.,"Koschmann and Bergendahl, 1968Longwell and others, 1965Robinson, J.P., 1996,  in Coyner, A.R., and Fahey, P.L., eds., Geology and ore deposits of the American Cordillera, 1995; symposium proceedings:  Reno, Geological Society of Nevada, v. 1, p. 567-579Wyman, R.V., 1987, in Johnson, J.
